    address?: InputMaybe<Scalars["Bytes"]>;

// @public (undocumented)

// @public (undocumented)
type MakeMaybe<T, K extends keyof T> = Omit<T, K> & {
    [SubKey in K]: Maybe<T[SubKey]>;
};

// @public (undocumented)
type MakeOptional<T, K extends keyof T> = Omit<T, K> & {
    [SubKey in K]?: Maybe<T[SubKey]>;
};

// @public (undocumented)
type Maybe<T> = T | null;
